  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_311b9fb1-9aa1-4582-82b2-f8ff29c3034b'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<div id="review_893002563" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/893002563" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/893002563?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18924472-sweet-filthy-boy">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer893002563" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4041282283125126465"><b>4.5 Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/a73dfafc-8f0f-40cb-9ffd-23818f2dad92_zps7451d24f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399972697i/9616298.jpg' alt=' photo a73dfafc-8f0f-40cb-9ffd-23818f2dad92_zps7451d24f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Sweet Filthy Boy</i> was one of those books that sucked me in from the very beginning. Sweet, sexy and hilarious, it was a real winner in my book! I love books that make me laugh, have heroines I actually like, and boys that make me swoon. This book had all three of those elements. <br/><br/>Mia Holland is a recent college graduate. She has one weekend. One weekend to let loose, be free before the responsibilities her father has placed on her go in to effect. She’s expected to go to business s</span>
  <span id="freeText4041282283125126465" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/a73dfafc-8f0f-40cb-9ffd-23818f2dad92_zps7451d24f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399972697i/9616298.jpg" alt=" photo a73dfafc-8f0f-40cb-9ffd-23818f2dad92_zps7451d24f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Sweet Filthy Boy</i> was one of those books that sucked me in from the very beginning. Sweet, sexy and hilarious, it was a real winner in my book! I love books that make me laugh, have heroines I actually like, and boys that make me swoon. This book had all three of those elements. <br><br>Mia Holland is a recent college graduate. She has one weekend. One weekend to let loose, be free before the responsibilities her father has placed on her go in to effect. She’s expected to go to business school in Boston. She’s not sure thats what she wants, but she doesn’t know what else she would do. While on vacation, she does something thats not normal for her. She goes outside of her comfort zone. She takes a chance. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/190469b5-3069-431e-bfd0-93f9979342ef_zpsf40cc969.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399972697i/9616299.jpg" alt=" photo 190469b5-3069-431e-bfd0-93f9979342ef_zpsf40cc969.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Meeting Ansel Guillaume, an attorney from France, will change everything. Mia is quiet, a little shy and not forthcoming. With Ansel, everything is different. She can talk, be herself, even her friends are shocked. Ansel just has this way about him. He makes her feel special. <br><i>
  <blockquote>He makes me feel like I’m the only person on the planet. He looks at me like he’s one second away from devouring me.</blockquote>
</i> <a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/d9023d10-8a22-46bc-9087-b626b0612235_zps4e0b0473.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399972697i/9616300.jpg" alt=" photo d9023d10-8a22-46bc-9087-b626b0612235_zps4e0b0473.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ansel and Mia’s one night together is wild and spontaneous. And after a lot of contemplation, it leads Mia into taking the plunge. For once, she will do what she wants, not whats expected of her. She is going to spend the summer in Paris with Ansel. At first, it’s not what she expected. Ansel is working a lot and she is doing a lot of sightseeing. Things between them is something they’ve never been before. A little awkward. As a little time passes, Mia and Ansel find a way to move past that awkward stage and slowly fall into the summer of ‘like’.<br><br>I loved Mia and Ansel together. Loved them! Mia was fantastic. By the end of the story, I was so proud of her and the strength she developed. And her friends. OMG. I loved them both and I’m so happy we will be getting more books from this group. The Whore Jar- cracks me up! Then there was Ansel. ADORED that boy! He was so charming, sweet and swoony. I want to listen to him speak some french! I loved both characters individually, but most of all- I loved them together. And the things they brought out in one another. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I’m lost in you.” <br>“Me too.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/5d1339e9-76c4-4490-abdb-5d7bbddcb61e_zpsad5f44d5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399972697i/9616301.jpg" alt=" photo 5d1339e9-76c4-4490-abdb-5d7bbddcb61e_zpsad5f44d5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Yes. I just want to fall asleep inside you. Maybe our bodies will make love again when our brains sleep.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Ansel and Mia’s chemistry was off the charts. This might sound like an odd thing to say, but some of the more fun and creative sex scenes were my favorite part of the story! They were sexy, sure, but they also made me smile. If you are looking for a book that will make you laugh, make you grin, make you feel good and has that sweet and sexy romance vibe with some fabulously lovable characters, check this one out! <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/c99e58a5-0b2f-4fe2-82a7-1ce18eeb5672_zps3a7da512.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399972697i/9616302.jpg" alt=" photo c99e58a5-0b2f-4fe2-82a7-1ce18eeb5672_zps3a7da512.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Life is built of these little horrible moments and the giant expanses of awesome in between.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/baf85b63-8908-4a56-943c-845f9d2d7e80_zps6fb3767d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399972697i/9616303.jpg" alt=" photo baf85b63-8908-4a56-943c-845f9d2d7e80_zps6fb3767d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=conquer-my-tbr-in-2015">conquer-my-tbr-in-2015</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer914327985" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12720256185859465505">HOT DAMN!! The writing duo of Christina Lauren created another <i>panty-melter.</i> I read book 2, Dirty Rowdy Thing, first and then this one. I know, sometimes I’m backwards! :)<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Viva Las Vegas!</u>
</b><br/>I love books that at some point the characters end up in Vegas because you’re guaranteed for some crazy antics. And this book didn’t disappoint in that area. Mia and Ansel have just met and done something crazy that leads to Mia spending the summer with Ansel in his city, Paris. Who does that? Meets a guy and</span>
  <span id="freeText12720256185859465505" style="display:none">HOT DAMN!! The writing duo of Christina Lauren created another <i>panty-melter.</i> I read book 2, Dirty Rowdy Thing, first and then this one. I know, sometimes I’m backwards! :)<br><br><b>
  <u>Viva Las Vegas!</u>
</b><br>I love books that at some point the characters end up in Vegas because you’re guaranteed for some crazy antics. And this book didn’t disappoint in that area. Mia and Ansel have just met and done something crazy that leads to Mia spending the summer with Ansel in his city, Paris. Who does that? Meets a guy and then spends a summer living with him 5,000 miles away?!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432424637i/14957405._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Did the authors read my diary?</u>
</b><br>Oh wait! That would be me who meets a guy who lives 3,000 miles away while in college and then flies across the country to spend the summer with him. Like Mia I was in my early twenties when I decided to be <i> wild and free</i> for the summer! Btw, that guy I spent the summer with followed me back home, after the summer, and we’ve been married 20 years in September. So, I totally understood Mia’s need to escape from family and life pressures and just go be someone else for a few months. <i>My teens better not be reading this review because I won’t be supporting them if they decide to follow in their parents footsteps. *lol*</i><br><br><b>
  <u>Naughty student and the Professor!,</u>
</b><br>All their roleplaying foreplay was S.T.E.A.M.Y. Seriously, I loved watching them get into character and let their awkwardness melt away. It was a great way to learn more about each other without having to have a sit down conversation. Especially since Ansley was forced to work the majority of the time Mia was visiting. He’s an upcoming lawyer who is aspiring to get ahead on the case he was working on so he could have the pick of jobs. <br><br><b>
  <u>Avoidance… never the answer.</u>
</b><br>Ansley has a past he’s been avoiding telling Mia about because he’s afraid it will ruin their future. And, at the same time, Mia is escaping from the realities of her life: broken relationship with her dad, her career ending injury, and not wanting to continue her education by getting a Master’s degree. When all those things bubble to the surface they are no longer able to live in denial. They are forced to take responsibility for their actions. <br><br><b>Sweet Filthy Boy</b> was a book that worked for me. It was sweet but not cheesy . . . it was steamy but not erotica. Just an all around fun romantic book. I’m looking forward to Oliver’s book that comes out in the Fall<b> but</b> now that I know about Perry, I’m dying to see how the authors' work that story into an HEA. <br><br>Don't forget to check out the novella that tells Ansel's point of view of the <i>morning after.</i> It's an audio for $1.95-&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1BhfHTT">http://amzn.to/1BhfHTT</a><br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18775297.Sweet_Filthy_Boy__Wild_Seasons___1_" title="Sweet Filthy Boy (Wild Seasons, #1) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1395723782s/18775297.jpg" alt="Sweet Filthy Boy (Wild Seasons, #1) by Christina Lauren" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21411902.Dirty_Rowdy_Thing__Wild_Seasons___2_" title="Dirty Rowdy Thing (Wild Seasons, #2) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1397738746s/21411902.jpg" alt="Dirty Rowdy Thing (Wild Seasons, #2) by Christina Lauren" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21942340.Dark_Wild_Night__Wild_Seasons___3_" title="Dark Wild Night (Wild Seasons, #3) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1428713287s/21942340.jpg" alt="Dark Wild Night (Wild Seasons, #3) by Christina Lauren" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/930111390?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=choke-dat-ho">choke-dat-ho</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer930111390" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6461286988815643257"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br/><br/>[2 star beginning<br/>4.5 star story<br/>3 star ending]<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399598051i/9572690._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I do not read “light, sweet, & funny” books. To be honest, those bore me and I need stories with much more depth so I avoided the Beautiful Bastard series. This book, however, caught my attention. At first glance the blurb is quite simplistic and sounds like any other book but I had this nagging feeling there was a hidden layer to the story and I was right! (Sorry not going to tell you – you’ll just have to read and find out!)<br/><br/><u>2 star beginnin</u></span>
  <span id="freeText6461286988815643257" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br><br>[2 star beginning<br>4.5 star story<br>3 star ending]<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399598051i/9572690._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I do not read “light, sweet, &amp; funny” books. To be honest, those bore me and I need stories with much more depth so I avoided the Beautiful Bastard series. This book, however, caught my attention. At first glance the blurb is quite simplistic and sounds like any other book but I had this nagging feeling there was a hidden layer to the story and I was right! (Sorry not going to tell you – you’ll just have to read and find out!)<br><br><u>2 star beginning</u><br><br>I’m all for total escapism because that’s why I read; however, I need <i>some</i> kind of realism in there as well or I won’t be able to relate to the characters at all. This beginning was quite ludicrous – I was staring at my book in disbelief at what was happening. If it weren’t for a friend warning me about the unrealistic first 25% I would’ve stopped reading. I have no doubt this part will appeal to longtime fans of this dynamic author duo and anyone else looking for some hot fun. Call me pragmatic or whatever, but it’s way too impulsive and careless for my tastes. <br><br><u>4.5 star story</u><br><br>After Mia hops on a plane and goes with Ansel to Paris, the story took a turn for the better and I absolutely adored it! I’d say hot sex takes up about 70% of the book but it was done so, so well! I pretty much laughed my ass off with Mia and Ansel’s role playing (TONS of that going on hehe) and despite the rather unbelievable start to their relationship, I liked that they took some time to get to know each other – those scenes were so awkward but funny to read!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399598051i/9572691._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>3 star ending</u><br><br>Everything – the story, the steamy sex scenes, etc…- was going so well and then BAM, plot twist and I pretty much disliked Ansel after that. To clarify, deliberately omitting information from your significant other is called lying in my book (and this is something big too). I did like how Mia finally took charge and grew a backbone, and though the ending was a bit rushed and tied up too nicely, it was also very sentimental and touching so overall I liked it. <br><br>As this is the first book I’ve read from these authors and, for the most part, liked, I’m not opposed to reading the next one in the series. My biggest complaint would be the ridiculous first 25% of the story but I do realize without it, there wouldn’t be the rest of the story which was significantly better. If you end up struggling with the beginning like I did, keep reading! It’s worth it. <br><br><i>ARC provided by <u>Gallery Books</u> via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.</i><br></span>

<div id="review_769161058" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/769161058?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer769161058" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16715977860589039244">4.5--<b>Ansel Loving</b>--Stars!!<br/><br/>Yep, even when he was stupid I LOVED Ansel! <br/><br/>And what can I say...I love a good weekend in Vegas story! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393219353ra/8678422.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Look....it's Ansel, Finn and Oliver.<br/><br/>What happens when you have 3 hot chicks + 3 hot guys + sluts on a trampoline???<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400522247ra/9684965.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Dumb shit like <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[get married <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>!!! But can I just tell you how happy that made me!!<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“I want to love all of my life as much as I love this night.”</blockquote>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434531ra/877104.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So some crazy things happened in Vegas....this happened to be Mia and Ansel's stor</span>
  <span id="freeText16715977860589039244" style="display:none">4.5--<b>Ansel Loving</b>--Stars!!<br><br>Yep, even when he was stupid I LOVED Ansel! <br><br>And what can I say...I love a good weekend in Vegas story! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1393219353ra/8678422.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Look....it's Ansel, Finn and Oliver.<br><br>What happens when you have 3 hot chicks + 3 hot guys + sluts on a trampoline???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400522247ra/9684965.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dumb shit like <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[get married <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>!!! But can I just tell you how happy that made me!!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I want to love all of my life as much as I love this night.”</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380434531ra/877104.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So some crazy things happened in Vegas....this happened to be Mia and Ansel's story. Mia and her friends have graduated from college and are in Vegas for one last hoorah!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400523923ra/9685059.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mia and company hook up with Ansel and company and so the story goes. <br><br>In every day life Mia is shy, she's quiet, she can come off as aloof. Ansel brings something out in her. Mia is set to start business school in the fall, much to her dismay. It's not at all what she wants to do with her life. And meeting Ansel might just change things for her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395108228ra/8947576.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After their weekend in Vegas, Mia agrees to spend the summer with Ansel in Paris. A chance to explore a beautiful city. <br><br>Mia and Ansel kind of started backwards. This summer was their chance to get to know each other, to fall in love, to discover each other.<br><br>I seriously fell in love with Ansel. I loved Mia. I loved how they fell in love. I loved how hard they fell. I loved how they grew. I loved how they laughed. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381215794ra/4547802.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everything was just so perfect. Until it wasn't....Ansel you stupid, stupid boy!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400523923ra/9685060.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Withholding information, misleading Mia....shame on you! <br><br>It's okay though....I forgive you!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400523923ra/9685061.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What can I say? I loved the Bastard series and I loved this one. It had great characters, great banter and SUPER HOT sex! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399246516ra/9526014.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2467761976763131106"> 4 HOT STARS<br/><br/>I loved it! Sweet Filthy boy was funny, sexy and cute! I think the title for the book, totally fit with the male characters personality. Ansel was amazing, he captivated me and I'm sure he will steal your hearts when you finally meet him to! What I loved more in this book like in Beautiful Players is that her characters are so real, they are not perfect they have their problems like us in our every day life!! <br/><br/>The story begins with Mia who is in Las Vegas with her friends for vacation</span>
  <span id="freeText2467761976763131106" style="display:none"> 4 HOT STARS<br><br>I loved it! Sweet Filthy boy was funny, sexy and cute! I think the title for the book, totally fit with the male characters personality. Ansel was amazing, he captivated me and I'm sure he will steal your hearts when you finally meet him to! What I loved more in this book like in Beautiful Players is that her characters are so real, they are not perfect they have their problems like us in our every day life!! <br><br>The story begins with Mia who is in Las Vegas with her friends for vacation after graduating college and before moving to Boston. In Vegas Mia meets Ansel a Frenchman who instantly catches her eyes. There is an immediatelconnection between them, and something extreme happens that will change their lives... <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399595143i/9572392._SX540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mia must decide if she will go to France with Ansel for the summer.. Must she follow her head or her heart?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399859670ra/9603528.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She goes with her heart and she decides to visit France,<br>and they start a relationship based on sex..<br>But is the sex enough to make their relationship last?<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399859670ra/9603529.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think I must go to France *sigh* Ansel was amazing! He was funny, sweet, charming, filthy and impulsive! I loved him! I'm going to buy the audiobook too, I want to listen him speaking French Mia was shy and she has to deal with a lot of things... Ansel was there for her and helped her to deal with some of them! But sometimes she pissed me off and I want to slap her! The plot was interesting with funny moments! The were a lot of sex scenes and they were so hot!!<br>If you are a fan of the Beautiful Bastard series I'm sure you will love it <br>and <br>If you are looking for a SWEET FILTHY BOY this is what you need!<br> <br><br><br> <a href="http://readmore-sleepless.blogspot.gr/" rel="nofollow noopener"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394736264i/8898096.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>*ARC kindly provided by Galley Books via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review*</a></span>

My brain can't understand what happened.</i><br/><br/><a href='http://s1334.photobucket.com/user/ariestibet/media/587885_zpsd2dfc7cf.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText2809577874219254021" style="display:none"><i>I just can't believe what I just read. I really want to think that the last 17 days I spent struggling. Trying to finish this book. All. Everything. Was a nightmare. But it wasn't. The book exist and I did finish reading it. My brain can't understand what happened.</i><br><br><a href="http://s1334.photobucket.com/user/ariestibet/media/587885_zpsd2dfc7cf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389311551ra/8018651.gif" alt="boring photo 587885_zpsd2dfc7cf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>This ain't my first Christina Lauren's book, but I'm thinking it might be my last.</b><br><br> What to say? Where to begin?<br><br>The storyline. I don't believe there was one here and before you say anything, yes I need to bring the BB series to this conversation. From the BB series I only LOVE "Beautiful Bastard" and "Beautiful Player." The other books weren't that good. As soon as Christina Lauren announced "The Wild Seasons Series" I told myself this would be different. The last book from the BB series ( "Beautiful Beginning" ) was such a disappointment to me, I really NEEDED this book to be AWESOME! <br><br><a href="http://s1334.photobucket.com/user/ariestibet/media/785893_zpse912642a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388154042ra/7749814.gif" alt="happy photo 785893_zpse912642a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It wasn't. <br><br><a href="http://s1334.photobucket.com/user/ariestibet/media/611112_zpse620c0c8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Let's start with the characters. None of them were likable. None of them were adorable. Actually Ansel and Mia were very annoying. I didn't feel the connection between reader and characters and even less the connection between the characters.<br><br><a href="http://s1334.photobucket.com/user/ariestibet/media/tumblr_mcr4isqyIE1r9uv98o1_400_zps86f13c98.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394218367ra/8823622.gif" alt="crying photo tumblr_mcr4isqyIE1r9uv98o1_400_zps86f13c98.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Like I said before, STORYLINE? There just wasn't any. And the hints of some sort of plot were so much predictable. So EXTREMELY Obvious. I wanted to cry. Or maybe I should be happy. Because now I know I'm a psychic. I knew what was going to happen before it actually happened.<br><br>Back to the Book : I struggled with it a lot and there was more sex than story. I don't mind the sex scenes, but when the sex scenes bored you to death as well, that's when you know something is not OK with this book.<br><br><a href="http://s1334.photobucket.com/user/ariestibet/media/tumblr_mi55jmCT7k1rhg5lso9_500_zpsb0c1c0af.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I did skip a few paragraphs here and there and I feel I didn't miss anything important.<br><br>I wanted to LOVE this series. That won't happen.<br><br><a href="http://s1334.photobucket.com/user/ariestibet/media/8935439_zps78b22a7b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer1421360829672910276"><b>4.5 <i>Filthy Boy</i> Stars</b><br/><br/>You know those stories were people go to Vegas, get drunk, get married, and then get it annulled? Yeah, this isn’t one of the stories or at least not the full story. <br/><br/>Mia and her girlfriends have just graduated college and to celebrate they go to Vegas. While in Vegas they meet three sexy men all from other countries. Ansel, Finn and Oliver are the trifecta of hotness and when they all get drunk, one thing leads to another, and they end up paired up and married. Finn, Harlow, </span>
  <span id="freeText1421360829672910276" style="display:none"><b>4.5 <i>Filthy Boy</i> Stars</b><br><br>You know those stories were people go to Vegas, get drunk, get married, and then get it annulled? Yeah, this isn’t one of the stories or at least not the full story. <br><br>Mia and her girlfriends have just graduated college and to celebrate they go to Vegas. While in Vegas they meet three sexy men all from other countries. Ansel, Finn and Oliver are the trifecta of hotness and when they all get drunk, one thing leads to another, and they end up paired up and married. Finn, Harlow, Oliver, and Lola do the expected thing and get their marriages annulled. But not Ansel and Mia, they decide to stay married. <br><br>Mia’s life changed forever when her dancing career ended tragically, now she is living the life her father wants for her. So when she meets Ansel and he makes her feel alive and happy for the first time since dancing, she doesn’t want to give that up…at least drunk Mia insist that she doesn’t.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415749238i/11840083._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ansel is the sweetest guy and he falls quickly. So when drunken Mia proposes to him and begs to stay married to her even after they sober up and realize it was a mistake…he does.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415749238i/11840084._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The next morning their trip is over and it’s time to say goodbye, but Ansel isn’t ready to say goodbye and asks Mia to accompany him to Paris for the summer. When a <i>Sweet Filthy Boy</i> asks you to go to Paris for the summer, there is really only one answer. Yes, please. <br><br>This story is so cute and sweet. I loved reading about Ansel and Mia. While getting together was pretty crazy, their real relationship shaped up nicely. The two of them have to learn how to coexist in the real world, and get to know the each other. This story is appropriately named because Ansel is the sweetest boy with the dirtiest of ways. This is quick sexy read that I highly recommend!<br><br><b>

  <span id="freeText14806364562834244385" style="display:none"><b> 4 filthy French stars </b><br><br><b> <i> “Life is built of these little horrible moments and the giant expanses of awesome in between.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/sweetfilthyboycollage.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b> Sweet Filthy Boy </b> starts off with a bang, in which Mia our heroine, takes a graduation trip to Vegas where she meets a sexy frenchman Ansel, and the two get married. Mia ends up following Ansel to France, where he returns to work and is hardly around. Mia finds herself mostly alone, in a foreign land, when she decides to make the most of her summer in Paris and with Ansel. <br><br>Mia spends most of her time looking at famous places like the Luxembourg Gardens: <br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/sfbluxgardens.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>(^^^Holy crap I need to get my ass back to Paris, I missed this when I was there!)<br><br>And the Eiffel Tower:<br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/eiftow.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>^^^Geez, Mia had it sooooooooo rough in France. NOT!!<br><br>Anyways, I gotta say I loved me some Ansel. He was far from perfect, but he <b> tried </b>. Ansel did his best to make things work out, and although he made some shitty decisions, his intentions were always for what he thought was best for his and Mia's marriage.<br><br><b> <i> “He’s the guy who’ll do a ridiculous robot dance to make you laugh, who’ll lick the tip of your nose, make a fool out of himself for a smile. I’m sure if I tried to wrestle him to the ground, he’d let me win. And enjoy every minute.” </i> </b><br><br>The instalove thing didn't bother me that much, because that's what I come to expect from a guilty-pleasure read like this one. Also, I don't really consider it instalove because the characters struggled throughout the entire book to connect with each other and tried to take the time to get to know each other. <br><br><b> <i> “I want to love all of my life as much as I love this night.” </i> </b><br><br>My main issue with this book? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The role-playing. Ugh, nothing makes me cringe worse than role playing. Sorry guys, this is a personal preference and I made ick faces when it happened. I did my best to overlook it. I understand the point that the author was trying to make, where Mia had to pretend to be someone else to be comfortable with herself, but I could have done without. The only thing worse than role-playing would be if she called him "daddy" and praise Jesus she did not do that!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The pacing of the book was off. Near the middle of the book I started to get bored. And by bored I mean the entire middle of the book was about Mia and Ansel having sex, and to be honest, I started to lose interest. When a book is driven by sex scenes and not by the characters, that's when I want to quit. It's the biggest issue that I had with Beautiful Bastard; too much sex, not enough plot. Luckily, the beginning and end of this book was actually about the plot and driven by the characters, so it was a success in my book. <br><br>I do feel the big reveal should have happened a lot earlier on in the book because the ending felt very rushed and could have had more of a smooth transition. I'd also like to know <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ if Mia and Ansel really can make it work, it was very unclear to me about that at the end, long term future I mean  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br>Overall, this exceeded my expectations because I <b> hated </b> Beautiful bastard, so bravo to the writing team that is Christina Lauren. Wonderful job ladies! </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14457130-whitney-atkinson?shelf=smutty">smutty</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2481378905" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13219979807651695591">4.5 stars<br/><br/>Despite this book's unfortunate title and cover art, it's actually really good. The bad boy vibe that the whole aesthetic sets up is completely wrong--the love interest of this book is actually so cute and sweet and gentle and I would have never picked this book up had Emily not told me it was her fav by Christina Lauren.<br/><br/>Overall, solid book. It's perhaps one of the smuttiest I've ever read, but it still somehow has room to develop the characters and a plot. That it's set in Paris is als</span>
  <span id="freeText13219979807651695591" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />Despite this book's unfortunate title and cover art, it's actually really good. The bad boy vibe that the whole aesthetic sets up is completely wrong--the love interest of this book is actually so cute and sweet and gentle and I would have never picked this book up had Emily not told me it was her fav by Christina Lauren.<br /><br />Overall, solid book. It's perhaps one of the smuttiest I've ever read, but it still somehow has room to develop the characters and a plot. That it's set in Paris is also a perk. The reason I took .5 stars off is because it just didn't have anything that grabbed me personally. Usually with books I smash the 5-star button on, something about the characters and plot really clicks with me, like how I could relate to the main character. But this just lacked that quality, maybe because the characters made decisions and took risks that I would never. It's hard to get into specifics because it's spoilery, but a couple of the plot decisions were bothersome because from a personal preference standpoint, I just don't find them interesting or compelling ways to create conflict. <br /><br />One gripe I have with Christina Lauren books is that there's always a drunk sex scene where the MC forgets what happened, and I find it so annoying. It's consensual and everything so there's no issue there, but it comes off as sooo unromantic to me for her to wake up and just be like "wild night lol!!!!! anyway" Again, this fits into the fact that this book doesn't completely satisfy my preferences for a book to be a perfect romance, so it might not bug anyone else.<br /><br />(parts of this reminded me of warnette, but we don't have to talk about it.)<br /><br />I would definitely recommend this though if you want a change from books with super macho masculine dudes. It's very steamy yet real and cute, and it inspired me to start learning French on Duolingo.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1826968337836649831"><b>5 I love French Men Stars</b><br/><br/>Sweet Filthy Boy is a standalone and is part of the Wild Seasons series. I read the books out of order. I was really curious about Ansel since all my friends loved him and he’s mentioned a few times in the future books. I can honestly say, he’s my favorite Hero of the series.<br/><br/>Nothing is sexier than a French man.<br/><br/>This will be an audio review.<br/><br/>I will do the audio versions of this series because it’s really good. Sadly this is from Mia’s POV, so I don’t get a male narrator, bu</span>
  <span id="freeText1826968337836649831" style="display:none"><b>5 I love French Men Stars</b><br><br>Sweet Filthy Boy is a standalone and is part of the Wild Seasons series. I read the books out of order. I was really curious about Ansel since all my friends loved him and he’s mentioned a few times in the future books. I can honestly say, he’s my favorite Hero of the series.<br><br>Nothing is sexier than a French man.<br><br>This will be an audio review.<br><br>I will do the audio versions of this series because it’s really good. Sadly this is from Mia’s POV, so I don’t get a male narrator, but there is a mini-novella / audio only book just with Ansel’s voice, so not is all loss. <br><br>One word to describe this book is kinky sex and lots of it. I wouldn’t have it any other way.<br><br>Mia and her friends go to Las Vegas. She wanted to have fun and relax, but when wakes up from a night out she realizes she is married. Yes, I love random marriages books. I love love love love this plot! Mia wants to end the marriage, but Ansel said he wouldn’t until after the summer.<br><br>Who is Ansel? He’s a sexy French man with a heart of gold. Ansel needs to go back to France for the summer and wants Mia to join him. Mia does. <br><br>I thought Mia was fun, level-headed and very adventurous. I loved that she threw caution to the wind and followed her heart. It was really cute reading the interactions between Ansel and Mia because they are husband and wife, but they are also strangers. Ansel is sexy and he works hard. He works all hours of the day, but he tries his best to be there for Mia since she is alone in the country. Even though it’s a female narrator doing the voice, I loved it when she spoke in Ansel’s voice. Her fake French accent was adorable. <br><br>Throughout the marriage Mia tries hard to engage more with Ansel and be adventurous in bed. She dresses up in different outfits and it’s really cute when she tries to seduce her husband. I would consider this book more erotica. <br><br>Overall, Sweet Filthy Boy was a fun, sexy read and it’s my favorite out of the series. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18775297.Sweet_Filthy_Boy__Wild_Seasons___1_" title="Sweet Filthy Boy (Wild Seasons, #1) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1395723782s/18775297.jpg" alt="Sweet Filthy Boy (Wild Seasons, #1) by Christina Lauren" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://amzn.to/1RSWAHf" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br></span>

</b><br><br>The story starts with the wild weekend in Vegas where Mia and her friends decide to celebrate their graduation. Mia carries lot of baggage of her past and unsure future but that weekend she decides to let go of her life and for once wanted to be somebody else not tied up by burden of being a responsible daughter. Her wild side sees the light of day when she lays her eyes on Ansel. He is gorgeous and charming with hot body and there's undeniable attraction between them. <br><br><b>

Living room, or bed, or floor, or bed, 				or wall, or mirror, or bar, or floor?” <br><br> “Shhh,” I whisper, lifting my cup to					 take another, more careful sip of coffee. 				I smile into my mug. “You’re weird.” <br><br>“I think I need a cast for my penis.” </i>
</b><br><br>Here’s when the story gets interesting, while Lola and Harlow (Mia’s friends) annul their marriage with Oliver and Finn (Ansel’s friends) Ansel convinces Mia to give their marriage a try and to spend the summer with him in Paris. Sounds crazy right!? Marrying a complete stranger and to top that follow him to Paris, but with Ansel she actually feels alive, he makes her brave, wild and seductive. She wants to relive this life before she follows the path her father wanted for her. <br><br><b>

</b><br><br>Escaping to Paris and extending her fling brings both of them together, they push the boundary of their sexual life which change the direction of their growing relationship. What starts as fun and careless transforms to something strong and meaningful. That summer changes both their life, even Ansel the most impulsive and fun loving is also struggling to right his past and have a normal life, but when Mia finally considers to remain married to Ansel his past threatens their future.<br><br>Will Mia forgive him for hiding the truth? Was that the reason he asked her to spend summer in Paris so as to redeem himself? What happens when this adventure ends?<br><br>This was surprisingly a good read, it was blend of funny, sexy, dirty and passionate romance. It had me smiling and swooning most of the time. What I loved more was the strong friendship Mia and her friends share, can’t wait to read their story.<br><br>I would love to rate higher if it was not for tons of sexual encounters taking huge space in the middle of the story, not complaining about the hotness here ladies but wish it was plot driven. Though the ending was sweet it felt rushed. All in all enjoyed this sweet filthy Story of discovering oneself.<br><br><i>P.S: Thanks for the recommendation Yasmine x!</i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15489668708139630915"><b> 3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b> I get so frustrated with these books because the endings just simply aren't satisfying for me. I really enjoy them otherwise, so that is where the frustration stems from. I always enjoy Ms. Lauren's characters and storylines (and her sex scenes aren't bad either *wink, wink*), but her endings just leave me wanting. I want a solid HEA! I want to see them succeeding in their dream careers together as a healthy functioning couple!! Other than the ending, I actually enjoy</span>
  <span id="freeText15489668708139630915" style="display:none"><b> 3.5 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b> I get so frustrated with these books because the endings just simply aren't satisfying for me. I really enjoy them otherwise, so that is where the frustration stems from. I always enjoy Ms. Lauren's characters and storylines (and her sex scenes aren't bad either *wink, wink*), but her endings just leave me wanting. I want a solid HEA! I want to see them succeeding in their dream careers together as a healthy functioning couple!! Other than the ending, I actually enjoyed this more than I thought I would. I had this book in my tbr pile for a while now, but I always put it off. I think the "boy" part of the title conflicted with my self conscious or something -- because I always want my H's to be manly! I didn't find that the H was immature though. I actually enjoyed their story, so I'm happy that I gave it a shot :)<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Mia and Ansel's story. They meet in Vegas with their friends at a bar. They are instantly drawn to one another, and wake up after a crazy night married to one another. Mia takes a gamble and decides to follow Ansel back to Paris for the summer and to give their marriage a shot. There are some hot sexy times, some unexpected real world obstacles, and some ex drama...but they do get a HFN ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was told in Mia's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good until the abrupt ending. I never skimmed and it flowed well otherwise.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Kind of. They have an instant connection and instalust, but no mention or internal thought of love until later.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 3 stars. Ansel. I liked him, but then he did disappoint me with not being completely upfront with Mia.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4 stars. Mia. I liked her. I liked how she stepped outside of her box and how she jumped right in with Ansel.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b> Low, no tissues needed.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Not much <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h does push away at one point because of a fight they have. The H is the main pursuer of the relationship. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Moderate/high. They have some hot chemistry and scenes, but there were times (only a few) where it seemed like the sex scenes took over the storyline. <br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> Yes. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Condoms are used until std checks are done, and birth control is discussed as well. I don't remember any mention of previous practices. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H has an ex that causes some drama for the couple.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b>No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H does say that he cheated on his ex in his past.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ They are separated for what I think is around 2 weeks. There is no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b> Not really<br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had way too an abrupt ending for me. Why do you always do this to me, Ms. Lauren?!? I always seem to feel underwhelmed with her endings, but I keep on reading them...obviously ;). I would call this a HFN ending because there were some big unanswered questions left. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are married still and have decided to stay that way<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I guess...because the h <i>had</i> asked her friend to get in touch with a lawyer for her regarding an annulment close to end that wasn't addressed again -- so like I said, unanswered questions... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I got it with my scribed subscription.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This should be <u>Safe</u> for most readers.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the h pushing the H away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a ~2 week (I think) separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a HEA ending IMO (see above) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

</blockquote><br /><b>Genre:</b> New Adult Romance.<br /><b>Cover:</b> 8/10<br /><b>Writing:</b> 9/10<br /><b>Heroine:</b> 6/10<br /><b>Hero:</b> 9/10<br /><b>Hotness:</b> 8/10<br /><b>Romance:</b> 9/10<br /><b>Extra book Details:</b> Heroine POV. stand alone. 304 kindle pages.<br /><br />Mia has just finished college, she's leaving for Business School in Boston in three weeks, much to her father's pleasure and her despair.<br />Her best friends Harlow and Lola encourage her to lose herself at a weekend in Las Vegas.<br />Only problem she ends up losing herself in Ansel, the French Adonis who makes her melt from the other side of the room. <br /><br />- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -<br /><br /><b>The heroine had a lot of hang-ups. For the first 30-40% she seemed to constantly be suffering with some kind of angst. Anything from stuttering, nerves, panic, guilt, worry, humiliation, her confidence, body hang ups, sex hang ups, worrying about her father, her future...</b> It greatly lessened after that, I was really grateful that it did. But it seemed to stunt her personality somehow.<br /><br /><b>That was my ONLY negative.</b><br /><br /><b>Yip, Ansel was totally Sweet and nice, and totally flirty and Filthy.</b> Also totally impulsive. A real 'seize the day' kind of man who <i>'falls a little bit in love with everything that he sees.'</i> I really truly loved him.<br /><br />I loved seeing Mia's best friends and Ansel's best friends together, they were really fun and seemed to have a lot of personality. There wasn't much of this interaction though, very little in fact.<br /><br /><b>All in all, a less angst heroine with more personality and AN EPILOGUE, would have made this a 5 star.<br />So more like 4.5 stars.</b><br /><br />*ARC received by Netgalley*</span>

<div id="review_2932681689" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2932681689" />
    <a title="preoccupiedbybooks" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36310974-preoccupiedbybooks"><img alt="preoccupiedbybooks" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577647566p2/36310974.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2932681689?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="preoccupiedbybooks" class="user" itemprop="url" name="preoccupiedbybooks" href="/user/show/36310974-preoccupiedbybooks">preoccupiedbybooks</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781476751818" href="/book/show/18870399-sweet-filthy-boy">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2932681689" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16149406531188735691"><b>I wanted some classic Christina Lauren, but what I actually got was more smut than story...</b><br/><br/>Firstly I could tell that this one was written a while ago, as this was nothing like the duos more recent offerings! Nowadays <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6556689.Christina_Lauren' title='Christina Lauren' rel='nofollow noopener'>Christina Lauren</a> write romantic type chick-lit, with a few sex scenes but they mostly fade to black. This book was most definitely more in the new adult genre. Now I'm not one to shy away from a steamy sex scene, and I'm not really a fan of skipping over the details, but this one ha</span>
  <span id="freeText16149406531188735691" style="display:none"><b>I wanted some classic Christina Lauren, but what I actually got was more smut than story...</b><br /><br />Firstly I could tell that this one was written a while ago, as this was nothing like the duos more recent offerings! Nowadays <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6556689.Christina_Lauren" title="Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Christina Lauren</a> write romantic type chick-lit, with a few sex scenes but they mostly fade to black. This book was most definitely more in the new adult genre. Now I'm not one to shy away from a steamy sex scene, and I'm not really a fan of skipping over the details, but this one had almost too much sex?! It was constant, and I felt myself rolling my eyes, bored, and started to skim read the sex scenes as there were <b>SO MANY!</b> This is definitely not a book to read in public! *blushes*<br /><br />I loved the setting in Paris, and wish we got to explore that more!<br />I loved Ansel as the love interest (when he wasn't having sex with Mia) as he was so sweet.<br />I liked the friendships both the characters had.<br />I liked the going off after college/uni and finding yourself for a bit, and think everyone should do that!<br />I actually liked both Ansel and Mia.<br /><br />These people did not get to know each other. There was very little in way of conversation or relationship. I wanted more about their background, I wanted them to share that in the book. They barely talked, except in some weird situations which I wont go into. I mean each to their own, but I think that if you're in a relationship, you have to be able to communicate, and if you can't, then you're not mature enough to have one.<br />The middle part of the book was odd. It dragged, and was just about the characters kind of avoiding reality by having constant sex in a myriad of different ways?!<br />There was quite a lot of what I would call violent sex. Bruises, bite marks, soreness etc. Sorry but that really doesn't do it for me, and I didn't expect it after reading quite a few of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6556689.Christina_Lauren" title="Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Christina Lauren</a>'s books now!<br /><br />To sum up, I liked the idea of this book, and maybe if it had been written more like their most recent novels, I would have liked it more. I wanted to see this couple get to know each other in more than a physical way. If you are looking for a quick smutty/porn read then go for it, no judgement, but this wasnt what I was looking for.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16149406531188735691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7119995098501593468"> <b>3.5 <u>Very</u> Sweet Stars</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413480455ra/11516984.gif' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It is a fact known, that once you get to Vegas. You tend to do something really Stupid. Regardless of what kind!, you just have to. (at least i did). >_>. And this <br/><i>Book</i> is the big example of what worst could happen when you visit Vegas for the weekend...<br/><br/><i>Sweet Filthy Boy.</i> it's about three ladies. who recently graduated from college, and looking for a quickie Vacation in Las Vegas before going back to REALITY!... <br/><br/>Mia Holland tries to cope with her sudden change reality. after</span>
  <span id="freeText7119995098501593468" style="display:none"> <b>3.5 <u>Very</u> Sweet Stars</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1413480455ra/11516984.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is a fact known, that once you get to Vegas. You tend to do something really Stupid. Regardless of what kind!, you just have to. (at least i did). &gt;_&gt;. And this <br><i>Book</i> is the big example of what worst could happen when you visit Vegas for the weekend...<br><br><i>Sweet Filthy Boy.</i> it's about three ladies. who recently graduated from college, and looking for a quickie Vacation in Las Vegas before going back to REALITY!... <br><br>Mia Holland tries to cope with her sudden change reality. after being badly injured in a car accident, her dream of dancing ballet shatters. and now she's not sure what she wants, with her stubborn Father who "forces" (in a way) her to go into Business School in Boston. So Mia's only escape/freedom is within these 3 days, with her besties. <br><br>While on Vacation, Mia goes outside of her comfort zone. Doing everything that she never usually does. and one of those is opening up to a random<br>Crème Brûlée french man Aka -&gt; Ansel Guillaume. who happens to be in US. spending time with his friends. Ansel's very charismatic, gorgeous,funny. <br><br>After having a wild,vague,crazy night together. Mia actually takes Ansel's offer and follow him to Paris. were she'll have a summer full of Dreams, and Fore Plays...<br><br>These two were like sex monkeys. <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391184ra/753367.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>You'll Witness all the above...<br><br>I really liked Ansel's goofiness. his carefree, he's easy to fall in love with, and couldn't blame Mia for you know what!!. But that last semi-realization that's what really got me angry toward Ansel! That was really stupid, yes?. Anyhow, I enjoyed reading this book, Although it's a bit to SWEET for me. <br><br> <br><br><b>
  <i>“Life is built of these little horrible moments and the giant expanses of awesome in between.”</i>

<span id="freeTextContainer535851651865628765"><b>4,5 Filthy Stars!</b><br/>	<br/>In a crazy weekend in Vegas, Mia meets Ansel. A sexy French guy who is vacationing with his friends. And in just one night they get to know each other and everything changes. They share things they didn’t shared with anyone else and something between them immediately starts to grow. <br/>In a impulse Ansel invites Mia to spend the summer in Paris with him and trying to run from her own life, Mia accepts. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400372498i/9668510._SY540_.jpg' width='350' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the beginning things are awkward. Ansel is always working and adaptation is</span>
  <span id="freeText535851651865628765" style="display:none"><b>4,5 Filthy Stars!</b><br>	<br>In a crazy weekend in Vegas, Mia meets Ansel. A sexy French guy who is vacationing with his friends. And in just one night they get to know each other and everything changes. They share things they didn’t shared with anyone else and something between them immediately starts to grow. <br>In a impulse Ansel invites Mia to spend the summer in Paris with him and trying to run from her own life, Mia accepts. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400372498i/9668510._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the beginning things are awkward. Ansel is always working and adaptation isn’t easy. But eventually they got past that and things get easy, and sweet (and sexy) again. But then real life kicks and they got to face it: They have opposite lives and live in different countries. Even in different continents.<br>So how can they stay together, if everything is set to make them apart from the beginning?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4,5 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> Original within its genre. Sweet, romantic and with pretty sexy moments. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First person, female POV. It was completely addictive. Heartwarming. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Mia was pretty good. She annoyed at some points, but I got past that pretty quickly. Ansel was great. And despite of one attitude of him I really didn’t like, he was a great hero.<br>The supportive characters were pretty good and I can’t wait to read their stories. 	<br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot!!<br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. But I needed a happier end. It felt too rushed.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_938805467" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/938805467" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/938805467?book_show_action=true">May 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13126896-michelle?shelf=01-signed">01-signed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer938805467" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14904807173664976070"><a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/14021127908' title='Screenshot_20 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400362179i/9667046.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='Screenshot_20' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Mia and her two besties, Harlow & Lola just graduated college and are off to Vegas to let loose & celebrate. But Mia's not the type of girl to just let it all go. Too much has happened in her past and the weight of the future she doesn't want to allow her to free, until she meets him. <br/><br/>Ansel is spending the last few days in Vegas before he has to head back to Paris and to his job as an attorney, one that does allow him much time for much else. Seeing Mia from across the crowded club, then kno</span>
  <span id="freeText14904807173664976070" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/14021127908" title="Screenshot_20 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400362179i/9667046.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="Screenshot_20" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Mia and her two besties, Harlow &amp; Lola just graduated college and are off to Vegas to let loose &amp; celebrate. But Mia's not the type of girl to just let it all go. Too much has happened in her past and the weight of the future she doesn't want to allow her to free, until she meets him. <br><br>Ansel is spending the last few days in Vegas before he has to head back to Paris and to his job as an attorney, one that does allow him much time for much else. Seeing Mia from across the crowded club, then knocking at his door was all it took to get this boy hooked. <br><br>Mia finds herself completely at ease in his presence, the stuttering is non-existent - she can talk to him and tell him things that she never thought she'd say out loud, especially to a perfect stranger. When she decides to be bold and for one night be the girl that would never let a chance with a guy like this slip away, she discovers that she ends up with far more than she ever imagined.<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/14227948943" title="Screenshot_30 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400362179i/9667047.jpg" width="410" height="534" alt="Screenshot_30" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>One drunken night in Vegas turns into so much more. She knows the responsible thing to do would be to go home, prepare for the life she knows she doesn't want - but the idea of summer in Paris with Ansel, what girl could say no to that? <br><br><i>
  <b> "I want to love all my life as much as I love this night." </b>
</i> <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/92365175@N06/14207797845" title="Screenshot_32 by Charlie___Tango, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400362179i/9667048.jpg" width="400" height="488" alt="Screenshot_32" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sweet Filthy Boy was everything I wanted it to be. After coming of the success of the Beautiful Series I wasn't certain as to what to expect with their new series. But everything that I loved about their style was here. The trifecta of perfection, characters you love, a story that makes you swoon and writers that can make you laugh. <br><br><i>
  <b> "I'll be honest, from the looks of my mouth, I sucked dick for a long time last night." </b>
</i> <br><br>The way this duo writes these stories just amazes me. They hit the mark every time. The banter between the characters, the way the story line always remains clear - it just amazes me that this book, their stories come from two separate minds. <br><br><i>
  <b> "You just implied you're banging me tonight."<br>His grin gets bigger as his hands snake around my waist.<br>Play your cards right."<br>"I forgot my cards."<br>His smile wilts dramatically.<br>"But I did bring my penis."<br>"I'll try not to break it this time."<br>"In fact, I think you should try your hardest." </b>
</i> <br><br>There was a perfect balance to the lighthearted humor and the developing love story. The kind of love story where the characters have to work their way backwards from where they start to where they end. Falling in love with the idea of each other, without knowing one another. But knowing that the instant chemistry and the desire they feel is every bit real.<br><br> <i>
  <b> "With Ansel, I feel like my heartbeat is chasing his. I want to leave my fingerprints all over his neck and his lips. I want to suck on his skin, to see if it's as warm as it looks, and decide if I like what he was drinking by tasting it on his tongue. I want to have an entire conversation with him where I don't second-guess or struggle with a single word, and I want to take him back to the room with me and not use any words at all." </b>
</i> <br><br>There was always this tone of a much deeper story lingering just beneath the surface. There was humor, there was sizzling play time scenes and even some heartfelt moments - but there was a bigger picture of realizing what you really want in life and not being afraid to take it. Sometimes people find that path on their own, but sometimes it takes just finding the right person to show it to you.<br><br><i>
  <b> "Life is built of these little horrible moments and the giant expanses of awesome in between." </b>
</i> </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer932264594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9386067912524316700"><b>4 <i>Cerise</i> stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/image.jpg1_zps8elz5sum.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444443442i/16501730.jpg' alt=' photo image.jpg1_zps8elz5sum.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>"I want to love all of my life as much as I love this night."</blockquote>
</b><br/>I always find myself enjoying the work of these ladies. Witty banter, lovable main and side characters, and interesting situations will always be present. A rare miss for me, I found this to be a pretty solid read. <br/><br/>Immediately after college graduation, Mia and her two best friends head to Las Vegas for some fun, boozing it up, and possibly a one-night stand. <br/><br/>Ansel is also taking a break from stresses of reality. H</span>
  <span id="freeText9386067912524316700" style="display:none"><b>4 <i>Cerise</i> stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/image.jpg1_zps8elz5sum.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444443442i/16501730.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg1_zps8elz5sum.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I want to love all of my life as much as I love this night."</blockquote>
</b><br>I always find myself enjoying the work of these ladies. Witty banter, lovable main and side characters, and interesting situations will always be present. A rare miss for me, I found this to be a pretty solid read. <br><br>Immediately after college graduation, Mia and her two best friends head to Las Vegas for some fun, boozing it up, and possibly a one-night stand. <br><br>Ansel is also taking a break from stresses of reality. He is spending time in Sin City, away from France with his two friends as well. <br><br>Mia and Ansel meet, then meet again, and again. During their second night, the six strangers whoop it up. Mia cannot get over how comfortable she feels around Ansel. She is able to open up to him in many ways. It's too bad most moments shared are a little fuzzy due to the alcohol. <br><br>Upon waking the next morning, Mia finds that not only is she incredibly hungover, but apparently she's now married, based on the gold ring adorning her finger. <br><br>Ansel wants to make this marriage work and offers Mia the chance to come to France for the summer before heading back to school and a life she's dreading. Mia is hesitant, but can't deny that there is amazing chemistry with her new <i>husband</i>. <br><br><a href="http://s1278.photobucket.com/user/kabbaje6/media/Collages/imagejpg3_zpsdfa8f0b7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420627563i/13246214.jpg" alt=" photo imagejpg3_zpsdfa8f0b7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I liked this one a lot. I'm glad the situation was done in a realistic manner. They didn't have a perfect relationship, and actually had quite a few hurdles to overcome. Although I'm glad everything wasn't roses and daisies, I do think the tone of the book did a 180, and threw me off a little. <br><br>The beginning was very light and fun. I had laugh out loud moments with some of the things the girls and even the guys said. The two main characters obviously clicked, and their repartee was freaking adorable and funny. I guess I was a little surprised when the mood got kind of depressing after them being in Paris. I was still engaged, but they kind of fizzled some of their personalities, which given the circumstances is understandable. Ansel is a lawyer and would work constantly, so he was always gone. I felt for Mia, being alone in a strange city by herself, and having the only person she knows be aloof with her. Did this remind anyone else of the last two episodes of Sex in the City? I had major Carrie flashbacks. <br><br>This also had a great heat-factor, and I loved how Mia got them back on track in the sex department. If it wasn't for some of the things that came out in the beginning, I would've thought this was all they had going for them. So yeah, sometimes I did feel their relationship was primarily sex-based. They eventually did find this certain kink worked in helping them learn more about one another, and ending up helping them in the long run. <br><br>Overall I had periods of loving to just liking. Both MC's were incredibly endearing, and you were rooting for them the whole time. Towards the end, I simultaneously agreed and was annoyed by decisions that were made. I thought the resolution to their conflict was a little rushed, but I was able to overlook it and didn't think it damaged the story. <br><br>A fan of Christina Lauren, I will be checking out the other books in this series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9386067912524316700" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
