In fact, they explode... in bed. I can't imagine something hotter than gripping the headboard so hard, your knuckles turns white. <i>Plus the dirty french talk..</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399753403ra/9591739.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wasn't expecting a drama, actually. The authors were more into <i>'oh what is this feeling, im so confused'</i> thing as far as I can recall. Can you believe that this has yelling and crying, the works? Yes baby. There is. But don't worry. It doesn't cover half of the story. In fact, if I would do I pie chart, it'll be half-sex, 1/4 hilarious role-play, and 1/4 drama. *giggles*<br><br>Btw, can I just tell you that I'm not really a giggler? But Christina &amp; Lauren could always make me giggle since Bennett &amp; Chloe 'til now with Ansel &amp; Mia. Damn. Im totally hooked.<br><br>Aherm. So I recommend this to all beautiful and die-hard fans of Beautiful Bastard! This new series is the shit! Cross my heart.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405347499i/10384615.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*PRE-REVIEW*<br>It has the word <i>filthy</i> on it plus its from the authors of BB, then I'm in!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381579374ra/5062426.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12576102830906957131" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1108740698" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1108740698" />
    <a title="NinaReader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16299792-ninareader"><img alt="NinaReader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363276712p2/16299792.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1108740698?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NinaReader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NinaReader" href="/user/show/16299792-ninareader">NinaReader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781476751818" href="/book/show/18870399-sweet-filthy-boy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16299792-ninareader?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1108740698" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2262696103465808027"><pre>
  <b>5 Filthy, Sexy and Sweet Stars!!!</b>
</pre><br/>I am going to follow that rating up by saying that I’ve been and continue to be <b>
  <strong>
    <em>THE HUGEST CHRISTINA LAUREN FAN!</em>
  </strong>
</b><br/><br/>On the surface it’s a simple story about Ansel meeting Mia in Vegas. Mia and her two best friends are in Vegas celebrating their college graduation. Mia was a dancer but an accident now makes that impossible so she’s set for a course her father has chosen for her to attend Business school after the summer. <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416365688i/11943924.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In Vegas, she meets Ansel. Agai</span>
  <span id="freeText2262696103465808027" style="display:none"><pre>
  <b>5 Filthy, Sexy and Sweet Stars!!!</b>
</pre><br>I am going to follow that rating up by saying that I’ve been and continue to be <b>
  <strong>
    <em>THE HUGEST CHRISTINA LAUREN FAN!</em>
  </strong>
</b><br><br>On the surface it’s a simple story about Ansel meeting Mia in Vegas. Mia and her two best friends are in Vegas celebrating their college graduation. Mia was a dancer but an accident now makes that impossible so she’s set for a course her father has chosen for her to attend Business school after the summer. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416365688i/11943924.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In Vegas, she meets Ansel. Again on the surface, it’s just a super hot hook up but there are things that happen that pulls your heartstrings and want to see what could be with these two. <br>He’s leaving for home (Paris), she’s suppose to go back home to her parent’s house (San Diego) until school starts…to a future chosen for her, one she dreads. She's written herself a letter that reminds her of their night together. <b>
  <i>"I want to love all of my life as much as I love this night."</i>
</b><br><br>Then Ansel offers a summer with him and off we all go to Paris!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401808648i/9851321.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>
  <em>That being said, I’d like to introduce Ansel!!!!</em>
</strong><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416365689i/11943925._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is that sexy Frenchman fantasy you may already have and if you didn’t, you do now, come to life. <br>There’s plenty about Ansel that you’ll love. His accent, his thoughfulness, his easy going personality, and of course he's gorgeous and charming in that very Parisian way. We read about Ansel in his sexy suits, his jeans, his boxers, and (oh have mercy) in nothing at all. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416366036i/11943942.jpg" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>“It isn’t just that he’s gorgeous, and charming, it’s that he’s kind and thoughtful, and that it would never occur to him to be sharp or judgmental. There’s an inherent ease to him that’s disarming, and I have no doubt he leaves a trail of unintentionally broken hearts wherever he goes.”</i>
</b><br><br>This story is deceptive in it's simple plot. Just enough to tell the wonderful filthy and sweet story of Mia and Ansel. There are jems of sweetness, of caring and thoughtfulness and of course it's not a Christina Lauren book without making you laugh out loud. Also again as with their Beautiful series of book, there's plenty of hot sex (wow the role playing)...in this case described as filthy sex and I loved every filthy word of it! <br><br>The summer of fun turns into something real and the story is very character driven. There's a realism and rawness to their relationship that makes you fully invested in them. Everything isn't always smooth but what you do know is how they belong together. The writing is one of my favorites (I can't say it enough). Personally for me I can read a hundred of these books and be in reading bliss. It's my own favorite style of writing, I love the characters, I love the plot, it's funny and fun, but underneath the seemingly simple fun plot is a second layer of depth of a wonderful love story. <br><br>Christina Lauren gave me everything I want in a book (again)!<br><br><b>Awesome Quotes:</b><br><b>
  <i>"I'm sorry my body is sort of...hard to please."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"Remind me again why we didn't take my car?"<br>"Because it smells of Coppertone and dubious choices?"</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"The asshole is French."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"Which was your favorite? Living room, or bed, or floor, or bed, or wall, or mirror, or bar, or floor?"</i>
</b><br><b>
  <i>"I think I need a cast for my penis."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"Stay", he interrupts in a tight whisper. "I'm dreading the day you leave. I'm losing my mind thinking about it."</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I know it isn't my job to make sure she's okay anymore. But if what she feels for me is even a fraction of what I feel for you, I want to be careful with her heart, because I can't imagine what I would do if you left me. It would wreck me."<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442436720i/16233973._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2262696103465808027" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('BERwxN/pNhj/TITx0PCTSLHEkxG1EByL31NpwjT3wvK1manqs3OOtJKgqWBIAOq6ukvjbZM5XIxnBlEDd/jHkA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wM84i9buyISFM42qVXntHkL07TUkBezn82uccUtgMOZxEuGlunRwKOjfoDvNiZTsSXudSQIsrOBLPqSwCG81hA==')})
  }
